<script>
    function DVWebNodeAssetError(name, assetUrl) {
        window.ueLogError && window.ueLogError(new Error('Failed to load ' + assetUrl), {logLevel: 'ERROR', attribution: 'DVWebNode:assets'});
        window.ue && window.ue.count('DVWebNodeAssetsError', 1);
        var ext = assetUrl && assetUrl.split('.').pop().split(/\#|\?/)[0];
        window.ue && window.ue.count('DVWebNodeAssetsError' + name + ext, 1);

        var evt = null;
        if (typeof window.CustomEvent !== 'function' ) {
            var params = { bubbles: false, cancelable: false, detail: { name: name, assetUrl: assetUrl } };
            evt = document.createEvent('CustomEvent');
            evt.initCustomEvent('DVWebNodeAssetError', params.bubbles, params.cancelable, params.detail);
        } else {
            evt = new CustomEvent('DVWebNodeAssetError', { detail: { name: name, assetUrl: assetUrl } });
        }
        
        evt && window.dispatchEvent(evt);
    }
